 gahane khareednaa ek mahangaa shauk he, aise main unhen sahi tareeke se sahejnaa bahut jaruri he
 If you want, you can adopt these measures
 ye behad saral upaay hai jinase aapke gahane lambey samay tak achche or nae bane rahenge
 1
 mahange gahanon ko ham kisi khaas avasar par hi pahante hai
 In such a situation, as soon as the party is over and you return home, immediately remove those ornaments and keep them in a safe place
 isse unke khone kaa dar bhi nahin rah jaataa or dabakar tuutane kii ashanka bhi nahin rah jaati he
 2
 kai baar aisa hota he ki ham jaldbaaji main gahanon ko unki asal shape ke anusaar na rakhkar kisi bhi tarah rakh dete hai
 But the ornaments should be kept on the basis of their shape
 jaise necoles ho to use modakar rakhane ke bajaay jeweler dwaara die gaye box main rakhana behatar hoga
 3
 stone kii jewelery ko chote-chote silk paauch main rakhana behatar hota he
 Stones are protected by doing so
 4
 Clean the jewelry before placing it in the box
 halke haathon se jewelery ko coton se pochh len
 By doing this, the dust particles on it will be cleaned
 5
 Periodically check the jewelery

 It will be safe to do so
